< Text>
My favorite store in the world!
I absolutely LOOOOVE this store!  I love the clothing, the jewelry, accessories, the home decorations, candles, crystals, music, incense, I am not kidding - such a HUGE selection of awesome items - Absolutely everything in here I adore!  The vibe in here is incredible - so soothing and fun at the same time.  Reena, the owner is one of the kindest souls on earth.  She will help you find the perfect outfit or anything you are looking for.  I have bought gifts for my friends and family and they always love whatever I buy from here.  Reena cooks up delicious food and hosts an event here twice a year with live music all day long.  Reena even helped me dress up in a sari - she taught me how to do it and now I can wear saris whenever I feel like dressing up.  If you're looking for unique, eclectic, vibrant, special items - this is the place to go!  I give this place 100 stars over and over again. Highly recommend< /Text>

<Rate>5<//Rate>< review>
Definitely recommend this place. We booked a reservation with less than 24 hours notice for a wedding party of 30-35 people and they accomdated us more than we could have ever asked for. We weren't expecting a private room or anything, just tables to fit all of us after the  ceremony. In addition to the private room, they set it up to make it look as elegant as possible - linen table cloths, flowers in vases, and tables setup in a large square to make it look more like a reception dinner instead of a last minute reservation. The bartender Luis was the one I spoke to on the phone and he was so helpful in getting it setup for us and making sure we were happy with everything. He went out of his way and made sure everything was perfect for us. Not only that, we had excellent service from our waitresses and quick service from the kitchen in getting our food and drinks to us. We really couldn't have even imagined a better dinner there. We are so grateful and appreciate everything the staff at Echo did for us. Everyone loved how it turned out and we were all in awe of how awesome it turned out to be with last minute plannings. They went above and beyond and we would definitely recommend this place!< /review>

<rating>3</rating>< review>
Went on a friday night with some friends. Atmosphere was nice. Sat outside on their patio and listened to the live DJ. Service was excellent and friendly. The thing that brought down my score was my food. I ended up getting the french dip. Im not surprised that it was 15 bucks for my meal as it seems every place in tahoe seems to jack their prices up due to their expensive resort town status. However for that price i would expect to get more than just a tiny basket of fries.  The au jus sauce was the nail in the coffin though. It was so bland! And despite that fact, I was considering myself lucky that the sandwich alone was pretty good because they only supplied enough bland au jus to supply half the sandwich. I'd come back if i had to, but id rather try out a few other places before that happens.< /review>

<Review>My wife and I stayed at Lake Tahoe Resort in early June/17 and had dinner twice at their Echo restaurant.  Nice place, friendly staff, clean, and not a crowded set up with the tables/booths.  A good variety of food offerings.  Fair priced compared to similar restaurants in the area but the best thing is that there is no driving involved.
If you like ahi tuna steak seared and served raw you MUST have it there.  It was laid over a bed of rice cake/risotto with Asian slaw topped with thin slices of ginger.  The sauce they used over the ahi was absolutely delicious.  I always order seared ahi whenever it is on any menu but I have to say this was the absolute by far best I've ever had.  Wife had a delicious grilled chicken breast dish which she totally enjoyed.
The next night we decided to have burgers and thought we'd go to one of those restaurants nearby but then checked out the natural grass fed burgers at Echo and decided why would we go to a sports type bar restaurant when we can get better meat at a place as nice as Echo.  Fair priced and delicious burgers!!< /Review>< pics>

<rating>4<//rating>< review>
I realize each worker's case load is maxed out and they may seem slow. But with sec 8 everything is a process, if feel they are neglecting your case, you have the right to submitt in writing your concern and drop it in the box...I have found that they will respond within 3 or 4 days. And for those 911 case's. You can go up stairs and request to see your worker. It may take a minute but you will get in to see them. I prefer to be the first one in the AM and ussually I'm seen within 15 minutes or so. Anytime past that and you have better packed a lunch. As far as being on the list we all know it's long, but there are places that can move you to the top of the list. Remember, they are not going to tell you who they are. The Vet's, Pact, Mental Health, Catholic Charitys, Father Joe's. It's up to you to do the footwork, don't fool yourselves thinking they are there to help you, their not, if you want something then YOU seek it out. SDHC will respect and honour that. Hope that helps. :-)<//review>
